Calcium channel blockers help relax the blood vessels, allowing more blood to move through them, according to WebMD.'

Prompt: 'What is the cause of Creutzfeldt-Jakob disease?\n' 
Generated text: '\nCreutzfeldt-Jakob disease (CJD) is caused by a brain-destroying protein called prion. Prion diseases are extremely rare and have no known cure.\n\nWhat causes Creutzfeldt-Jakob disease?\n\nResearchers have long known that prions are the cause of CJD. What they didn’t know was how the proteins are formed.\n\nFor years scientists have known that the protein is misfolded. But they didn’t understand how the misfolding occurs.\n\nIn a new study, a team of researchers from the University of Cambridge in England and the Wellcome Trust Sanger Institute in Hinxton, UK, discovered that the prions they studied are the result of a “breakdown” of a single amino acid.\n\nThey also discovered that this amino acid, called glycine, was being rapidly broken down in the brains of patients with CJD.\n\nThe researchers believe the discovery could help them develop new treatments for the disease.\n\nWhat are prions?\n\nPrions are a group of protein misfolding diseases that cause the death of brain cells. The most well-known prion diseases are scrapie and bovine spongiform encephalopathy (BSE), which is commonly called “mad cow disease.”\n\n“Prion diseases are extremely rare, and have no known cure. They appear to be the result of abnormal prion protein misfolding,” says Dr. Adrian James, a researcher at the Wellcome Trust Sanger Institute.\n\n“We discovered that prions are formed by the rapid degradation of a single amino acid, glycine, in brain tissue from patients with CJD.”\n\nThe researchers studied prions from both patients with CJD and from animals with a CJD-like disease called spongiform encephalopathies (SPE).\n\nSpongiform encephalopathies are a group of disorders that cause brain damage in animals. Prompt: 'What causes laryngitis besides cold or flu infection?\n' 
Generated text: '\nA:\n\nQuick Answer\n\nAccording to WebMD, several causes of laryngitis exist. Infections, including cold and flu, can be a cause of laryngitis, and so can allergies and irritations. Viral infections, such as the common cold, can cause swelling and irritation in the throat, resulting in laryngitis.\n\nKeep Learning\n\nInfluenza, or the common cold, is a viral infection that can cause inflammation of the throat and the larynx. The virus enters the body through the nose and then makes its way to the throat and larynx, causing sore throat and sneezing. Laryngitis can also be caused by allergies. Common allergies include seasonal allergies, hay fever and pet dander. Inhaling allergens through the nose causes irritation to the throat and the larynx, which can cause laryngitis.\n\nOther causes of laryngitis include a vocal cord infection, a condition called oropharyngeal candidiasis and bacterial infection. Infections of the larynx can cause swelling in the throat, and a vocal cord infection can cause a sore throat and sore larynx. Bacterial infections, such as tonsillitis and laryngitis, are caused by bacteria that enter the body through the throat and the larynx. In some cases, bacteria can also cause scarring in the throat, which can make breathing difficult.\n\nLaryngitis can also be caused by irritated or inflamed tissue, which can be caused by a number of things. Irritation can be caused by smoking, poor oral hygiene or excessive smoking, chronic asthma, chronic bronchitis, emphysema and chronic bronchitis, as well as certain medications, according to WebMD.'

The immune system attacks and inflames the protective myelin sheath that coats your nerves. This damages the nerves and disrupts your ability to control your muscles, including your vision and balance.\n\nMS is an unpredictable disease that affects people of all ages and races. It is more common in young adults and women than in men.\n\nWhat causes multiple sclerosis?\n\nScientists don’t know the cause of MS, but they think several factors contribute. Bronchitis causes shortness of breath, chest pain and coughing, and it is often accompanied by a persistent cold. Treatment with antibiotics is typically prescribed.\n\nSymptoms of bronchiolitis are similar to those of chronic bronchitis. Generated text: '\nA:\n\nQuick Answer\n\nHigh blood pressure is a common medical condition in which the force of the blood pumping through the arteries is too high, causing damage to the walls of the arteries. To find out if you have high blood pressure, your doctor will take a complete medical history and examine you for any unusual symptoms.\n\nKeep Learning\n\nYour doctor will perform a blood pressure test, also called a blood pressure reading, to determine your blood pressure. The blood pressure test uses a cuff that is attached to an arm or leg and inflated to determine your blood pressure. The cuff then is inflated to a specific level for a certain amount of time, usually five minutes. After the cuff is deflated, the pressure is recorded and compared to a healthy blood pressure.\n\nYour doctor may also perform other tests, such as blood work or an echocardiogram, to determine if you have high blood pressure. The diagnosis may require that your doctor check your blood pressure several times over the course of several days or weeks.'

Prompt: 'What are the benefits of reducing blood pressure?\n' 
Generated text: '\nDoctors say that high blood pressure contributes to the risk of heart disease, strokes, kidney failure, and other serious medical conditions. The primary goal of treatment for high blood pressure is to reduce the force of the blood against the walls of the arteries, preventing the hardening of the arteries, reducing the risk of heart disease, and preventing blood from leaking into the spaces between the heart and the lungs. Treatment options for high blood pressure include lifestyle changes, blood pressure medications, and when necessary, a combination of both.\n\nLifestyle changes\n\nLifestyle changes are a primary way of lowering blood pressure. Health professionals encourage individuals to make changes to their diet, regular exercise, and weight. They also encourage individuals to drink enough water, limit alcohol, and avoid smoking. In addition, health professionals encourage individuals to follow a healthy sleep schedule. People who have high blood pressure should avoid sleeping for 12 hours or more a day.\n\nBlood pressure medications\n\nDoctors may prescribe blood pressure medications to individuals with high blood pressure. They may use medications for individuals who do not respond to lifestyle changes. Doctors may prescribe medication for more than one individual with high blood pressure. Some people have high blood pressure that fluctuates or changes over time. Drugs may be used to stabilize blood pressure.\n\nCombination of blood pressure medications\n\nDoctors may prescribe combination blood pressure medications to individuals with high blood pressure. These medications may include diuretics and angiotensin receptor blockers. Doctors may prescribe these medications for more than one individual with high blood pressure. Diuretics help the kidneys eliminate salt from the body. Angiotensin receptor blockers help constrict the blood vessels and reduce blood pressure.\n\nIndividuals with high blood pressure should follow the advice of their health care professional. They should also be advised to follow any lifestyle changes and blood pressure medications that are recommended by their health care professional.'

Prompt: 'What is multiple sclerosis?\n' 
Generated text: '\nMultiple sclerosis is an illness that affects the nervous system. It’s a chronic condition that causes the brain and spinal cord to become damaged. This can lead to many different symptoms, which can include:\n\nNumbness\n\nTingling\n\nWeakness\n\nBlurred vision\n\nSlow movement\n\nProblems with balance\n\nFatigue\n\nBalance problems\n\nDizziness\n\nSpeech difficulties\n\nStroke-like episodes\n\nHeadaches\n\nIt’s often called the ‘brain’s immune system’ because it affects a part of the brain called the myelin sheath.\n\nThe myelin sheath is a fatty substance that surrounds nerve cells in the brain and spinal cord, protecting them. When multiple sclerosis damages the myelin sheath, nerve cells can’t communicate as quickly and clearly as they used to. This can result in problems with movement and co-ordination.\n\nIn the early stages of MS, the myelin sheath is damaged and we don’t yet know why or how this happens. As the disease progresses, the myelin sheath is damaged more and more, and the symptoms can become more severe.\n\nMS is the most common chronic neurological condition in Australia, with around 300 new cases diagnosed each year.\n\nHow can I tell if I have MS?\n\nThe signs and symptoms of MS are similar to many other conditions. It can be difficult to tell if you have MS without seeing your doctor. However, symptoms can be divided into:\n\nInvoluntary movements\n\nCognitive problems\n\nBalance problems\n\nSkin changes\n\nSensation problems\n\nTiredness\n\nYou can learn more about how to recognise the symptoms of MS here.\n\nIs MS contagious?\n\nMS is not contagious.\n\nHow can I manage my MS?\n\nTo help manage MS, it’s important to keep an active lifestyle. You should avoid being inactive for long periods, as this can cause physical and mental tiredness. You should also:\n\nGet plenty of rest\n\nDrink plenty of fluids\n\nEat a healthy, balanced diet\n\nGet enough sleep\n\nExercise regularly\n\nMake sure you have access to the latest information about MS\n\nBe aware of any symptoms you’re experiencing\n\nHow can I get support with MS?\n\nThere are many organisations that can help people with MS. These include support groups, specialist MS clinics, MS charities and health services.\n\nThe MS Society is Australia’s leading MS charity. Its mission is to fund research and provide support for people living with MS, their families and carers.\n\nThe National MS Society provides national MS support and services for people with MS and their families, including information, advocacy, health and disability services, education and employment support, and professional training.'

The doctor will ask the patient about their symptoms and may order a physical exam to confirm the diagnosis.\n\nKeep Learning\n\nThe doctor will first rule out other causes of the symptoms by evaluating the patient's blood and urine for abnormalities. The blood may be checked for immune system abnormalities, and the urine will be tested for genetic disorders. The doctor may perform a neurological exam, which involves checking the patient's reflexes and testing their coordination.\n\nThe doctor will typically diagnose multiple sclerosis based on a combination of the patient's medical history, clinical symptoms and neurological exam results. In addition, the doctor will check for other conditions that cause similar symptoms, such as an autoimmune condition.\n\nThe doctor will provide the patient with information about the cause of multiple sclerosis, including risk factors and ways to prevent the condition. The patient may be advised to take certain medications, such as beta-blockers, to control their symptoms and prevent future attacks."
